  <script type="application/javascript">
   var mobile_redirect = function() {
	return {
		is_touch: (('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.msMaxTouchPoints &gt; 0)),

		initializeRedirects : function () {
			var redirect = parseInt(this.readCookie('MobileOptOut')) != 1;
			var opt_out  = this.getUrlParam('MobileOptOut');

			if (opt_out) {
				switch (parseInt(opt_out)) {
					case 0:
						// Remove Session Opt Out
						document.cookie = "MobileOptOut=0; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-70 00:00:01 GMT; path=/;";

						redirect = true;
						break;
					case 1:
						// Session Opt Out
						document.cookie = "MobileOptOut=1; expires=0; path=/;";

						redirect = false;
						break;
					case 2:
						// Single Page Opt Out
						redirect = false;
						break;
				}
			}

			if (redirect === true &amp;&amp; this.isMobile()) {
				var url = false;
				var check = window.location.href;

				if (check.search('www.') != -1) {
					// Production Redirect

					url = check.replace(/:\/\/www\./i, '://m.');
				} else if (check.search('stores.') == -1) {
					// Rio Redirect

					url = url.replace(
						/(\.com\/|\.ca\/)/i,
						function (match, contents, offset, s) {
							return match + "mobile/";
						}
					);
				} else {
					// Other Redirect

					var part = check.match(/:\/\/([a-z]+)\d+-(v\d+)-(\w+)\./i);

					url = check.replace(part[0] + "marketlive.com", '://' + part[1] + ".uat.bbhosted.com");
				}

				if (document.referrer.length != 0) {
					url += (url.indexOf('?') != -1) ? '&amp;' : '?';
					url += 'udo_ref=' + encodeURIComponent(document.referrer);
				}

				window.location.href = url;
			}
		},

		isMobile : function () {
			var min_dim = Math.min(screen.availHeight, screen.availWidth);

			var is_mobile = (min_dim &lt; 700);

			if (!navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile/i)) {
				is_mobile = false
			}

			return is_mobile;
		},

		getUrlParam : function (name) {
			name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");

			var regexS = "[\\?&amp;]" + name + "=([^&amp;#]*)";
			var regex = new RegExp(regexS);
			var results = regex.exec(window.location.href);
			var result = false;

			if (results &amp;&amp; results.length &gt;= 1) {
				result = results[1];
			}

			return result;
		},

		readCookie : function(name) {
			var result = false;

			try {
				var name_eq = name + "=";
				var cookie = document.cookie.split(';');

				for (var i = 0; i &lt; cookie.length &amp;&amp; result === false; i++) {
					var c = cookie[i];

					value = c.split("=");
					if (value[0] == name) {
						result = '';
						for (var j = 1; j &lt; value.length; j ++) {
							result += (result.length == 0) ? "" : "=";
							result += value[j];
						}
					}
				}
			} catch (e) {
			}

			return result;
		}
	};
}();

mobile_redirect.initializeRedirects();
  </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var intl_timeout = false;

	jQuery($$('#intl_sites')).bind (
		'mouseout',
		function (event) {
			intl_timeout = window.setTimeout("$$('#intl_sites')[0].setAttribute('state', 'off')", .25 * 1000);
		}
	);

	jQuery($$('#intl_sites')).bind (
		'mouseover',
		function (event) {
			if (intl_timeout !== false) {
				window.clearTimeout(intl_timeout);
			}
		}
	);

	jQuery($$('*[kiosk="hide"]')).bind (
		(('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.msMaxTouchPoints &gt; 0)) ? 'click' : 'mouseover',
		function (event) {
			$$('#intl_sites')[0].setAttribute('state', 'on');
		}
	);

	function readCookie(name) {
		var name_eq = name + "=";
		var cookie = document.cookie.split(';');

		var result = false;

		for (var i = 0; i &lt; cookie.length; i++) {
			var c = cookie[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				c = c.substring(1, c.length);
			}

			if (c.indexOf(name_eq) == 0) {
				result =  c.substring(name_eq.length, c.length);
				i      = cookie.length;
			}
		}

		return result;
	}

	var kioskCookie = readCookie("kioskid");

	if (kioskCookie !== false &amp;&amp; kioskCookie != "") {
		jQuery($$('*[kiosk="hide"]')).css('display', 'none');
		$$('#toplinks')[0].style.top = "20px";
		$$('#toplinks &gt; table:first-child')[0].style.margin = "0px auto 0px auto";
	}
     </script>

   <script>
    var GlobalHeaderManager = {
	onTabHover : function(linkObj,tabId, tabCode,global_header){
	
		if(jQuery("#"+tabId+"_drop_down").length&lt;1){
			jQuery.ajax({
		        async : true,
		        type : 'GET',
		        url : '/customnavsubmenu.do?topnavcode='+tabCode,
		        success : function(data) {
					jQuery("#site_nav").append(data);
					global_header.toggleTab(linkObj);
				}
		    });
		}else{
			global_header.toggleTab(linkObj);
		}
	},
	loadTabUsingAjax : function(tabId,tabCode){
		if(jQuery("#site_nav &gt; #"+tabId+"_drop_down").length&lt;1){
			jQuery.ajax({
		        async : true,
		        type : 'GET',
		        url : '/customnavsubmenu.do?topnavcode='+tabCode,
		        success : function(data) {
					jQuery("#site_nav").append(data);
				}
		    });
		}
	}	
}
GlobalHeaderManager.loadTabUsingAjax('default_nav','Root Item Category for Site: PartyCity');GlobalHeaderManager.loadTabUsingAjax('cat5-1','5-1');GlobalHeaderManager.loadTabUsingAjax('cat5-5','5-5');GlobalHeaderManager.loadTabUsingAjax('cat5-4520','5-4520');
   </script>

            <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="leftFirstTd">
             <tr>
              <td id="photos_tab" valign="top">

            <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="leftSecTd">
             <tr>
              <td class="infoTabContent std_DetNewVideoLink" colspan="2" valign="top">
               <div id="newTabContent">
                <div id="photos_tab_content">
                 <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Open+Sans:400,700;" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
                 <!-- Alt / Title Tag Should be Populated with Site Sepecific Product Name -->
                 <div id="photos_tab_contents">
                  <img alt="Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit" itemprop="image" src="http://partycity2.scene7.com/is/image/PartyCity/598968?wid=300" title="Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit"/>
                 </div>
                 <link href="/includes/standard.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
                 <!-- HC should call halloweencity.scene7.com -->
                 <script language="javascript" src="http://partycity.scene7.com/s7viewers/html5/js/ZoomViewer.js" type="text/javascript">
                 </script>
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  function printHtmlPlayer(product_code, img_height, image_colspan) {
	var viewer = document.getElementById('photos_tab_contents');
	var innerHTML = viewer.innerHTML;

	try {
		//var mod    = &lt;?= ($this-&gt;config_var['qs'] ? 0.855 : 1 ) ?&gt;;
		//var mod    = (window.location.href.search('QuickViewEnhancement.do') == -1) ? 1 : 0.855;
		if (window.location.href.search('QuickViewEnhancement.do') != -1) {
			var mod  = 0.855;
		} else if (document.getElementById('verticalImageColumn')) {
			var mod = .75;
		} else {
			var mod = 1;
		}

		console.log("mod: "+mod);

		var ie_version = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE (\d)/i);

		if (!ie_version || ie_version[1] &gt; 8) {
			var w      = 400;
			var h      = 510;

			w *= mod;

			switch (img_height) {
				case 'taller':
				case 'tallest':
					if (mod == 1) {
						h = 640 * mod;
					} else {
						h *= mod;
					}
					break;
				default:
					h *=  mod;
					break;
			}

			viewer.style.height = h + 'px';
			var stage = w + "," + h;

			viewer.innerHTML = '';

			var config = {
				"containerId": "photos_tab_contents",
				"params": {
					"serverurl": "http://partycity.scene7.com/is/image/",
					"asset": "PartyCity/" + product_code + "_set",
					"iscommand": "qlt=100,1&amp;op_sharpen=0&amp;resMode=sharp2&amp;op_usm=1,1,6,0&amp;iccEmbed=0&amp;printRes=72",
					"stagesize": stage,
					"iconeffect": "0"
				},
				"handlers": {
					"initComplete": function() {
						//fixHtmlPlayerSetup();
					}
				}
			};

			var s7zoomviewer = new s7viewers.ZoomViewer(config);
			s7zoomviewer.init();
		} else {
			var w = 400;
			var h = 510;

			var flash_dim = 'ML_PDP_400_400';

			if (mod == 1) {
				switch (img_height) {
					case 'taller':
					case 'tallest':
						h = 640;
						flash_dim = 'ML_PDP_400_500';
						break;
				}
			} else {
				w = 340;
				h = 434;

				flash_dim = 'ML_PDP_340_434_v1';
			}

			viewer.style.height = h + 'px';
			viewer.innerHTML = '';

			// Build Flash Player
			obj_html = "&lt;object";

			var attr = {
				classid: "clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000",
				codebase: "http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,0,0",
				id: product_code + "_set",
				width: w,
				height: h
			};

			for (var field in attr) {
				obj_html += " " + field + "='" + attr[field] + "'";
			}
			obj_html += "&gt;";

			var attr = {
				allowScriptAccess: "Always",
				allowFulLScreen: "true",
				movie: "http://partycity.scene7.com/is-viewers-4.1/flash/genericzoom.swf?serverUrl=http://partycity.scene7.com/is/image/&amp;contentRoot=http://partycity.scene7.com%2fskins&amp;image=PartyCity/" + product_code + "_set&amp;config=PartyCity/" + flash_dim + "&amp;locale=en&amp;contentRoot=/skins/",
				menu: "false",
				quality: "high",
				scale: "noscale",
				salign: "LT",
				bgcolor: "#FFFFFF",
				wmode: "transparent"
			};

			for (var field in attr) {
				obj_html += "&lt;param name='" + field + "' value='" + attr[field] + "' /&gt;";
			}

			var attr = {
				wmode: "transparent",
				src: "http://partycity.scene7.com/is-viewers-4.1/flash/genericzoom.swf?serverUrl=http://partycity.scene7.com/is/image/&amp;contentRoot=http://partycity.scene7.com%2fskins&amp;image=PartyCity/" + product_code + "_set&amp;config=PartyCity/" + flash_dim + "&amp;locale=en&amp;contentRoot=/skins/",
				quality: "high",
				bgcolor: "#ffffff",
				swliveconnect: "true",
				allowscriptaccess: "always",
				name: product_code + "_set",
				type: "application/x-shockwave-flash",
				allowfullscreen: "true",
				pluginspage: "http://www.macromedia.com/go/getflashplayer",
				width: w,
				height: h
			};

			obj_html += "&lt;embed";
			for (var field in attr) {
				obj_html += " " + field + "='" + attr[field] + "'";
			}
			obj_html += " /&gt;&lt;/object&gt;";

			viewer.innerHTML = obj_html;
		}
	} catch (err) {
		viewer.innerHTML = innerHTML;
		console.log(err);
	}
}

		console.log("photos_tab_contents_divcontainer.style.top: " + new_top + "px :: " + mod);

		console.log(err);
	}
}

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      function styleLeftNav() {
		var nav = document.querySelector('td.navleftbg &gt; table[width="192"] &gt; tbody &gt; tr &gt; td');
		var span;

		for (var i = 0; i &lt; nav.childNodes.length; i ++) {
			if (nav.childNodes[i].nodeName == '#text' &amp;&amp; nav.childNodes[i].textContent.trim().length != 0) {
				span = document.createElement('span');
				span.className = 'nav_snippet';
				span.innerHTML = nav.childNodes[i].textContent.trim();

				if (span.innerHTML.search(/clearance|sale/i) != -1) {
					span.className += " clearance_snippet";
				}

				nav.insertBefore(span, nav.childNodes[i]);
				nav.removeChild(nav.childNodes[i + 1]);
			}
		}
	}

	styleLeftNav();
                     </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function readCookie(name) {
		var nameEQ = name + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
			if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
		}
		return null;
	}
	function eraseCookie(name) {
		createCookie(name,"",-1);
	}
	var orderCookie = readCookie("orderNumber");
	//alert("Kiosk Cookie " + kioskCookie );
	if (orderCookie != null &amp;&amp; orderCookie != "") {
		eraseCookie("orderNumber");

	}

	if (!readCookie('kioskid')) {
		var foresee = document.createElement('script');
		foresee.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
		foresee.setAttribute('src', '/text/partycity/foresee/foresee-trigger.js');

		document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].insertBefore(foresee, document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].childNodes[0]);
	}
       </script>

		js.src   = '/text/web-assets/slideshows/slideshow-shared/jquery-codeFree-sliding-seo-text.js ';
		js.type  = 'text/javascript';
		js.async = true;

		jQuery("&lt;link href='/text/web-assets/slideshows/slideshow-shared/family-page-style-990px-2015.css' rel='stylesheet' type='text/css'/&gt;").appendTo( 'head' )

		var script = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		script.parentNode.insertBefore(js, script);

		console.log('Family Copy Slider JS and CSS Added');
	}
}

         jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		regexS = "[\\?&amp;]code=([^&amp;#]*)";
		regex = new RegExp( regexS );
		results = regex.exec( window.location.href );

		if ( results != null ) {
			var coupon_code = results[1];
			coupon_code = coupon_code.toUpperCase();
			var coupon_file = '/text/coupon/coupon-email-' + coupon_code + '.html';
			if (coupon_code == 'PCX2ND' || coupon_code == 'PCXC4X') {
				PC_Pop('520','620', '', '', coupon_file,'','','close_on_outside_click','auto');
			}
		}
	});
        </script>

    function addToWishList(wishListAction) {
        var formObj = document.getElementById('mainForm');
        if (!(MarketLive.P2P.validateProductSelection(noQtyMsg, noOptionsMsg, formObj, 1)))
            return;

        formObj.action=wishListAction;
		formObj.target="";
        formObj.submit();
    }
	
    
    // Function to display personalization message if user has selected one or more personalized products
    function addToBasket(basket_form){
		 var flag = false;
        if (basket_form.isPersonalized != undefined)
        {
            for(i=0;i &lt; basket_form.isPersonalized.length;i++){
                if(basket_form.isPersonalized[i].checked){
                flag = true;
                break;
                }
            }
        }
        else if (basket_form.isPersonalized != undefined)
        {
            flag = basket_form.isPersonalized.checked;
        }       
        
        if (flag){
            if(!isPersonalizationConfigured){
                alert('Personalized products cannot be added to basket due to incomplete configuration.');
                return false;
            }
            else{
                //Place holder for action when user select atleast one personalized product
                //alert('You have selected an item that needs further personalization');
            }
        }
		 
		 if(MarketLive.P2P.validateProductSelection(noQtyMsg, noOptionsMsg, basket_form, 1,"true")){
			var mainForm = document.getElementById('mainForm');
			var action = "/addToBasketPopUp.do?method=addtobasket";
			// for TealiumAddToBasketSource the data is set in hidden field
			document.getElementById('addToBasketSourceData').value = sessionStorage.getItem("p2pSourceInfo");
			var familyPDPUrl = "false";
			var solrPoweredPDP = "true";
			var submitDataWithJSONForm = false;
			var  navPath=sessionStorage.getItem("p2pSourceInfo");
			if(familyPDPUrl == "true"){
				if (typeof(navPath) == 'undefined' || navPath.indexOf("Family QS") != -1) {
					submitDataWithJSONForm = false;
				}else{
				submitDataWithJSONForm = true;
				document.getElementById('pdpCollectionAddToBasketSource').value = "FAM|:";
				}
			}else if(true){
				submitDataWithJSONForm = true;
			}	
			if(submitDataWithJSONForm &amp;&amp; document.getElementById('pdpProductMapSize').value &gt;0){
				document.getElementById('pdpCollectionAddToBasketSource').value = "FAM|598968Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit";
				submitJSONForm(mainForm, action);
			}
			else{
				submitAddToBasketRequest(mainForm, action);
			}
			return false;
		 }

		 return false;
       // return validateProductSelection(noQtyMsg, noOptionsMsg, basket_form, 1,"true");
    }

function setQueryStringParam(basket_form){
	var currentLocation = location.href;
	if(currentLocation.indexOf("?") != -1){
		queryParam = currentLocation.substring(currentLocation.indexOf("?"));
		basket_form.detailPageQueryParam.value=queryParam;
	}
    return MarketLive.P2P.validateProductSelection(noQtyMsg, noOptionsMsg, basket_form, 1);
}

    function openPricePopup(priceurl, code){
        if(priceurl.length &gt; 0){
            window.open(priceurl + '?productcode=' + code,'_blank','height=450,width=600,scrollbars=1,resizable=yes');
        }else{
            alert('Configuration for this product is incomplete. Please select some other product.');
        }
    }

    jQuery("#photos_tab").click(function(){
				var pstr = jQuery("#photos_tab img:first-child").attr("src");
				var vstr = jQuery("#videos_tab img:first-child").attr("src");
				if(pstr.indexOf("_off")!=-1){
					pstr=pstr.replace("_off","_on");
					vstr=vstr.replace("_on","_off");
					jQuery("#photos_tab img:first-child").attr("src",pstr);
					jQuery("#videos_tab img:first-child").attr("src",vstr);
					jQuery("#videos_tab_content").css("display","none");
					jQuery("#photos_tab_content").css("display","block");
				}
			});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	//jQuery('#leftCol').css('min-height',jQuery('#leftFirstTd').innerHeight()+jQuery('#leftSecTd').innerHeight());
	var referrerURL = 'null';
	
	if(referrerURL.indexOf('multiProductAddToBasket.do')&gt;-1){
	 tealiumContentBasketSourceRender();

	}
	else {
		
		var navPath = sessionStorage.getItem("p2pSourceInfo");
		
		var currentLocation = location.href;
		var siteCodePath = tag_mgmt.udo_json.site_name+":"+tag_mgmt.udo_json.page_section_name+":"+tag_mgmt.udo_json.page_category_name+":"+tag_mgmt.udo_json.page_subcategory_name;
		
		if(typeof(navPath) != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; navPath != null) {
		    
			if(navPath.indexOf("QS") != -1) {
				
				navPath = navPath.substr(0,navPath.lastIndexOf(":QS"));
				if(navPath.indexOf("Directory") != -1) {
					navPath = navPath.replace("Directory QS","Directory QS PDP");
				}
				else if (navPath.indexOf("Search") != -1) {
					navPath = navPath.replace("Search QS","Search QS PDP");
					navPath = navPath.replace(":QS","");
					
				}
				else if (navPath.indexOf("RV QS") != -1) {
					navPath = navPath.replace("RV QS","RV QS PDP");
				}
				else if (navPath.indexOf("XSELL QS") != -1) {
					navPath = navPath.replace("XSELL QS","XSELL QS PDP");
					navPath = navPath.replace(":QS","");
					
				}
				else if (navPath.indexOf("Family QS") != -1) {
					navPath = navPath.replace("Family QS","Family QS PDP");
					navPath = navPath.replace(":QS","");
					
				}
				else if (navPath.indexOf("FAM QS") != -1) {
					window.console &amp;&amp; console.log('DEFAULTFM QS exist = '+navPath);
					navPath = navPath.replace("FAM QS","FAM QS PDP");
					navPath = navPath.replace(":QS","");
					window.console &amp;&amp; console.log('Updated navPath = '+navPath);
				}
				sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductCode","598968");
				sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductName","Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit");
				}
				else if(currentLocation.indexOf("refType=4") != -1) {
					navPath = "RV|"+sessionStorage.getItem("parentProductCode")+":598968|"+siteCodePath+":"+sessionStorage.getItem("parentProductName")+":Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit";
			   }else {
				
				  navPath = "PDP|598968#|"+siteCodePath+":Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit";
				  sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductCode","598968");
				  sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductName","Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit");
		        }
			
		}else{
			
			 navPath = "PDP|598968#|"+siteCodePath+":Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit";
			 sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductCode","598968");
			 sessionStorage.setItem("parentProductName","Day of the Dead Red Makeup Kit");
			
		  }

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function tpGCScroll(){
					var tpGC=jQuery("#topGCSection");
					if (jQuery(document).scrollTop()&gt;10 &amp;&amp; !tpGC.hasClass("topGCSection")){
						tpGC.addClass("topGCSection");
					}
					else if(jQuery(document).scrollTop()&lt; 10 &amp;&amp; tpGC.hasClass("topGCSection")){
						tpGC.removeClass("topGCSection");
					}
				}
				function tpGCScrollM(){
					var tpGC=jQuery("#topGCSection");
					if (jQuery(document).scrollTop()&gt;10){
						tpGC.css("top", (jQuery(document).scrollTop()-10)+"px");
					}
					else if(jQuery(document).scrollTop() &lt; 10){
						tpGC.removeAttr("style");
					}
				}
				if(typeof uagent === 'function' &amp;&amp; uagent()=="mobile"){
					jQuery(window).scroll(tpGCScrollM);
				} else {
					jQuery(window).scroll(tpGCScroll);
				}
  </script>
